<p>Before using this prompt, you need to create a new Nuxt project:</p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> nuxi@latest</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> init</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> hello-prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">cd</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> hello-prisma</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p>Once your Nuxt project is created, you can use the prompt below with your AI assistant to add Prisma and Prisma Postgres.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="how-to-use"><a data-card="" href="#how-to-use" class="peer">How to use</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Include this prompt in your AI assistant to guide consistent code generation for Nuxt + Prisma + Prisma Postgres projects.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>GitHub Copilot</strong>: Type <code>#&lt;filename&gt;</code> to reference the prompt file.</li>
<li><strong>Cursor</strong>: Use <code>@Files</code> and select your prompt file.</li>
<li><strong>Zed</strong>: Use <code>/file</code> followed by your prompt&#x27;s path.</li>
<li><strong>Windsurf</strong>: Use <code>@Files</code> and choose your prompt file from the list.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="prompt"><a data-card="" href="#prompt" class="peer">Prompt</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"># Specify the following for Cursor rules</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">description: Guidelines for writing Nuxt apps with Prisma Postgres</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">alwaysApply: false</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"># Bootstrap Nuxt app with Prisma Postgres (Prisma v7)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Purpose:**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Set up Prisma ORM with Prisma Postgres in a Nuxt project using the correct Prisma v7 patterns.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## FIRST: Check for an existing Nuxt project</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Before doing anything else, check whether the current directory already contains a Nuxt project by looking for </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`nuxt.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **If </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`nuxt.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> exists**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> → A project is already set up. Skip to &quot;Overview&quot; below.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **If the directory does NOT contain </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`nuxt.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> → Create a new project first:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> nuxi@latest</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> init</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> hello-prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">cd</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> hello-prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">After the project is created, verify </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`nuxt.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> exists before continuing.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">&gt; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Note**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">: This guide is updated for </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Prisma ORM 7**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">. Key changes from earlier versions:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">&gt; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `engine`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D"> property removed from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma.config.ts`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">&gt; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `url`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D"> removed from datasource in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`schema.prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D"> (now only in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">&gt; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D"> Use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@prisma/adapter-pg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D"> driver adapter for direct TCP connections</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">&gt; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `--no-engine`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D"> flag is no longer required for </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma generate`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">&gt; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D"> Requires Node.js 20.19+ and TypeScript 5.4.0+</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Overview of implementing Prisma with Nuxt</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Ensure a Nuxt project exists (see above)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Install Prisma and required dependencies (including dotenv and pg)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Initialize Prisma and configure schema</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Configure dotenv for environment variables</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create global Prisma client instance with Pg Adapter in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/utils/db.ts`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create Nuxt API routes using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`defineEventHandler`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create a Vue page to display data</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">8.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Add npm scripts for testing and database management</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">9.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create test script to verify setup</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## 🚨 CRITICAL INSTRUCTIONS FOR AI LANGUAGE MODELS 🚨</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">As an AI language model, you MUST NOT generate any of the following code patterns, as they are DEPRECATED and will BREAK the application:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ NEVER GENERATE THIS CODE - IT WILL BREAK THE APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;prisma-client-js&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">     // ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ NEVER USE default import location - IT WILL BREAK THE APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaClient } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &#x27;@prisma/client&#x27;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ WRONG IMPORT PATH - MISSING /client - IT WILL BREAK THE APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaClient } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../../prisma/generated&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ NEVER USE ACCELERATE - IT IS NOT USED IN THIS WORKFLOW</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { withAccelerate } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;@prisma/extension-accelerate&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"> // ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ NEVER USE accelerateUrl - IT WILL BREAK THE APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  accelerateUrl: process.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DATABASE_URL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION - use adapter</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">})</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ NEVER include url in datasource block - IT WILL BREAK THE APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">datasource db {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;postgresql&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  url      </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> env</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;DATABASE_URL&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION - moved to prisma.config.ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ NEVER include engine property - IT WILL BREAK THE APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> defineConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  engine: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;classic&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION - removed in Prisma v7</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">})</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ NEVER use Prisma Postgres HTTP URLs - ONLY use TCP URLs</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DATABASE_URL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;prisma+postgres://accelerate.prisma-data.net/...&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION - use postgres://</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ ALWAYS use standard TCP URLs:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DATABASE_URL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;postgres://...&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ✅ CORRECT</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ NEVER create PrismaClient without adapter - IT WILL BREAK THE APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()  </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ BREAKS APPLICATION</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Instead, you MUST ALWAYS generate ONLY this pattern:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ ALWAYS GENERATE THIS EXACT PATTERN</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;prisma-client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  output   </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;./generated&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ CRITICAL: MUST include /client at the end of import path</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaClient } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../../prisma/generated/client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaPg } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;@prisma/adapter-pg&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> pool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaPg</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ connectionString: process.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DATABASE_URL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">!</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> })</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> globalForPrisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> globalThis </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> |</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> undefined</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> globalForPrisma.prisma </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">??</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ adapter: pool })</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">if</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (process.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">NODE_ENV</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> !==</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;production&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) globalForPrisma.prisma </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { prisma }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## ABSOLUTE REQUIREMENTS FOR AI CODE GENERATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (not &quot;prisma-client-js&quot;)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST use custom output: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`output = &quot;./generated&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (relative to prisma directory)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@prisma/adapter-pg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> driver adapter with </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`PrismaPg`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/utils/db.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> as a global singleton instance (Nuxt auto-imports from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/utils/`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST wrap all database calls in try-catch blocks</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST import from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&#x27;../../prisma/generated/client&#x27;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (not </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&#x27;@prisma/client&#x27;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> or </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&#x27;../../prisma/generated&#x27;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`adapter`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> property in PrismaClient constructor</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">8.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST install </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`dotenv`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> and add </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import &quot;dotenv/config&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma.config.ts`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">9.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST add npm scripts for </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:test`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> and </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:studio`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to package.json</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">10.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST create a test script at </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`scripts/test-database.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to verify setup</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">11.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST NOT include </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`url`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in the datasource block of </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`schema.prisma`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">12.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST NOT include </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`engine`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> property in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma.config.ts`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">13.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`npx prisma init --db --output ./generated`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to create a real cloud database</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">14.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST use standard TCP URLs (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`postgres://...`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) in .env</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">15.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST NOT use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`accelerateUrl`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> or </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`withAccelerate`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">16.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST install </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`pg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> and </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@types/pg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> as dependencies</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## VERSION REQUIREMENTS</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Node.js**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: 20.19 or higher (Node.js 18 is NOT supported)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **TypeScript**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: 5.4.0 or higher (5.9.x recommended)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Prisma**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: 7.0.0 or higher</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT INSTALLATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Production dependencies</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> install</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> @prisma/client</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> @prisma/adapter-pg</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> pg</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> dotenv</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Dev dependencies</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> install</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> -D</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> @types/pg</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> tsx</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT PRISMA INITIALIZATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">&gt; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**FOR AI ASSISTANTS**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">: This command is </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**interactive**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D"> and requires user input. You </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**MUST ask the user to run this command manually**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D"> in their own terminal, then </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**wait for them to confirm completion**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D"> before proceeding with the next steps. Do NOT attempt to run this command yourself.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Initialize Prisma AND create a real Prisma Postgres cloud database</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> init</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> --db</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> --output</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> ./generated</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">This command:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Authenticates you with Prisma Console (if needed)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Prompts for </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**region**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> and </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**project name**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Creates a cloud Prisma Postgres database**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Generates:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">  -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `prisma/schema.prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (with correct output path)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">  -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `prisma.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (with dotenv import)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">  -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> with a </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`DATABASE_URL`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**IMPORTANT**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: Ensure the generated </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> uses a </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`postgres://`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> URL scheme. If it generates </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma+postgres://`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, replace it with the standard TCP connection string available in the Prisma Console.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```text</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">DATABASE_URL=&quot;postgres://...&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**IMPORTANT**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: Do NOT use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`npx prisma init`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> without </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`--db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> as this only creates local files without a database.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT PRISMA CONFIG (prisma.config.ts)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">When using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`npx prisma init --db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, the </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> is </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**auto-generated**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> with the correct configuration:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;dotenv/config&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ Auto-included by prisma init --db</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { defineConfig, env } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;prisma/config&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> defineConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  schema: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;prisma/schema.prisma&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  migrations: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    path: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;prisma/migrations&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    seed: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;tsx ./prisma/seed.ts&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ✅ NO engine property - removed in Prisma v7</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  datasource: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    url: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">env</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;DATABASE_URL&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Note**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: If you need to manually create this file, ensure </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import &quot;dotenv/config&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> is at the top.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT SCHEMA CONFIGURATION (prisma/schema.prisma)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Update the generated </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma/schema.prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> file:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  output   = &quot;./generated&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">datasource db {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider = &quot;postgresql&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  // ✅ NO url here - now configured in prisma.config.ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">model User {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id    Int     @id @default(autoincrement())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  email String  @unique</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  name  String?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  posts Post[]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">model Post {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        Int      @id @default(autoincrement())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  title     String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  content   String?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  published Boolean  @default(false)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  author    User?    @relation(fields: [authorId], references: [id])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  authorId  Int?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT GLOBAL PRISMA CLIENT</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/utils/db.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> file. Nuxt auto-imports exports from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/utils/`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, making </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> available in all server API routes without explicit imports:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaPg } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;@prisma/adapter-pg&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaClient } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../../prisma/generated/client&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ CRITICAL: Include /client</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> prismaClientSingleton</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> () </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> pool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaPg</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ connectionString: process.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DATABASE_URL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">!</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ adapter: pool });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">};</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClientSingleton</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> ReturnType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">typeof</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prismaClientSingleton&gt;;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> globalForPrisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> globalThis </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">  prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClientSingleton</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> |</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> undefined</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">};</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> globalForPrisma.prisma </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">??</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> prismaClientSingleton</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">if</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (process.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">NODE_ENV</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> !==</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;production&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) globalForPrisma.prisma </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## ADD NPM SCRIPTS TO PACKAGE.JSON</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Update your </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`package.json`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to include these scripts:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```json</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;scripts&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;build&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;nuxt build&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;dev&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;nuxt dev&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;generate&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;nuxt generate&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;preview&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;nuxt preview&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;postinstall&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;prisma generate &amp;&amp; nuxt prepare&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;db:test&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;tsx scripts/test-database.ts&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;db:studio&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;prisma studio&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CREATE TEST SCRIPT</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`scripts/test-database.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to verify your setup:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;dotenv/config&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ CRITICAL: Load environment variables</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaPg } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;@prisma/adapter-pg&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaClient } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../prisma/generated/client&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> pool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaPg</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ connectionString: process.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DATABASE_URL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">!</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ adapter: pool });</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> testDatabase</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;🔍 Testing Prisma Postgres connection...</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  try</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    // Test 1: Check connection</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;✅ Connected to database!&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    // Test 2: Create a test user</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">📝 Creating a test user...&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> newUser</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma.user.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">create</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      data: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        email: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;demo@example.com&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        name: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Demo User&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;✅ Created user:&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, newUser);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    // Test 3: Fetch all users</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">📋 Fetching all users...&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> allUsers</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma.user.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">findMany</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">`✅ Found ${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">allUsers</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">} user(s):`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    allUsers.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">forEach</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">((</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">user</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">`   - ${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">user</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">} (${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">user</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">})`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">🎉 All tests passed! Your database is working perfectly.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">catch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (error) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">error</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;❌ Error:&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, error);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    process.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">exit</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">testDatabase</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT API ROUTE IMPLEMENTATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Nuxt uses file-based API routing in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/api/`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">. The </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> instance is auto-imported from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/utils/db.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/api/users.get.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to fetch users:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> defineEventHandler</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> () </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  try</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> users</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma.user.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">findMany</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      include: { posts: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">true</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> users;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">catch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (error) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">error</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Error fetching users:&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, error);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    throw</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> createError</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      statusCode: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">500</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
