<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      statusMessage: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Failed to fetch users&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/api/users.post.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to create a user:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```typescript</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> defineEventHandler</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">event</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  try</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> body</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> readBody</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;{ </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> }&gt;(event);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    if</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">!</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">body.email) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">      throw</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> createError</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        statusCode: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">400</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        statusMessage: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Email is required&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> user</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma.user.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">create</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      data: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        name: body.name,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        email: body.email,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> user;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">catch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (error) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">error</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Error creating user:&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, error);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    throw</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> createError</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      statusCode: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">500</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      statusMessage: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Failed to create user&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CORRECT USAGE IN VUE PAGES</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Update </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`app.vue`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to display users from the database:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```html</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">template</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">h1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;Users&lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">h1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">ul</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> v-if</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;users?.length&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">li</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> v-for</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;user in users&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> :key</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;user.id&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        {{ user.name }} ({{ user.email }})</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">li</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">ul</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    &lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">p</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> v-else</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;No users yet.&lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">p</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  &lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">div</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">template</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">script</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> setup</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">data</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">users</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> useFetch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;/api/users&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;/</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">script</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## COMPLETE SETUP WORKFLOW</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">User should follow these steps (AI should provide these instructions):</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Ensure a Nuxt project exists**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> — check for </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`nuxt.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">. If missing, create one:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   npx nuxi@latest init hello-prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   cd hello-prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Install dependencies**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   npm install @prisma/client @prisma/adapter-pg pg dotenv</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   npm install -D prisma @types/pg tsx</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Initialize Prisma AND create Prisma Postgres database**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (⚠️ USER MUST RUN MANUALLY):</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">   &gt; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**AI ASSISTANT**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">: Ask the user to run this command in their own terminal. This is interactive and requires user input. Wait for the user to confirm completion before continuing.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   npx prisma init --db --output ./generated</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   The user should follow the terminal prompts to:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Authenticate with Prisma Console (if needed)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Choose a region (e.g., us-east-1)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Name your project</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   Once complete, this creates </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma/schema.prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, AND </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> with the </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`DATABASE_URL`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">   **User should confirm when done**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> so the AI can proceed with the next steps.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Verify </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> was created**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> — Ensure </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`DATABASE_URL`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> uses </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`postgres://`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">. If it uses </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma+postgres://`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, change it to the TCP connection string.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```text</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   DATABASE_URL=&quot;postgres://...&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">   **Do NOT invent or manually change this URL. Use the one from Prisma Console.**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Update </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`prisma/schema.prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> — Add the User and Post models (generator and datasource are already configured):</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   model User {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     id    Int     @id @default(autoincrement())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     email String  @unique</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     name  String?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     posts Post[]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   model Post {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     id        Int      @id @default(autoincrement())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     title     String</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     content   String?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     published Boolean  @default(false)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     author    User?    @relation(fields: [authorId], references: [id])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     authorId  Int?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`server/utils/db.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> with correct import path including </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`/client`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> and using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@prisma/adapter-pg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Add npm scripts**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`package.json`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> for </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:test`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:studio`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, and </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`postinstall`</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">8.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`scripts/test-database.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> test script</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">9.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Create API routes**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> — </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/api/users.get.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> and </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/api/users.post.ts`</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">10.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Update </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`app.vue`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to display users</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">11.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Push schema to database**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ```bash</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">12.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Generate Prisma Client**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    npx prisma generate</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">13.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Test the setup**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ```</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">14.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Start development server**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ```</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## AI MODEL VERIFICATION STEPS</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Before generating any code, you MUST verify:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Does the current directory contain </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`nuxt.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">? <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (not &quot;prisma-client-js&quot;)? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`output = &quot;./generated&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you importing from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`&#x27;../../prisma/generated/client&#x27;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (with </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`/client`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Did you add </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import &quot;dotenv/config&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Did you add </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import &quot;dotenv/config&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`scripts/test-database.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@prisma/adapter-pg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> with </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`PrismaPg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">8.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`adapter`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> property in PrismaClient constructor? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">9.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you wrapping database operations in try-catch? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">10.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Did you create the Prisma client in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/utils/db.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (not </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`lib/prisma.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">11.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Did you create the test script at </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`scripts/test-database.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">12.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Did you add </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:test`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> and </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:studio`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> scripts to package.json? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">13.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Did you remove </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`url`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> from the datasource block in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`schema.prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">? <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">14.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Did you remove </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`engine`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> property from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">? <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">15.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`npx prisma init --db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (not just </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`npx prisma init`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">16.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Is the DATABASE_URL a TCP URL (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`postgres://...`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)? If it&#x27;s a </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma+postgres://`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> URL, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">17.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Did Prisma generate the </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> file? If you invented the URL manually, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">18.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Are you using Nuxt auto-imports (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`defineEventHandler`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`readBody`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`createError`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)? If not, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## CONSEQUENCES OF INCORRECT IMPLEMENTATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">If you generate code using:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `prisma-client-js`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> provider → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**CLIENT GENERATION FAILS**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Wrong import path (missing </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`/client`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**MODULE NOT FOUND ERROR**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Missing </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import &quot;dotenv/config&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in prisma.config.ts → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**DATABASE_URL NOT FOUND ERROR**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Missing </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import &quot;dotenv/config&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in test scripts → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**ENVIRONMENT VARIABLE ERROR**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Default import from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@prisma/client`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**IMPORT ERROR**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`accelerateUrl`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> or </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`withAccelerate`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**UNNECESSARY ACCELERATE DEPENDENCY / CONFIG ERROR**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Missing custom output path → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**WRONG CLIENT GENERATED**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Including </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`url`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in datasource block → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**DEPRECATED CONFIGURATION ERROR**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Including </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`engine`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> property → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**DEPRECATED CONFIGURATION ERROR**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Using local URL (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`postgres://localhost:...`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**VERSION INCOMPATIBILITY ERRORS WITH Prisma v7**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`npx prisma init`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> without </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`--db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**NO DATABASE CREATED, ONLY LOCAL FILES**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Manually inventing DATABASE_URL → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**INVALID CONNECTION STRING ERRORS**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Creating client in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`lib/prisma.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> instead of </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/utils/db.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**NOT AUTO-IMPORTED IN NUXT SERVER ROUTES**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Missing </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`pg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> dependency → </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**ADAPTER INITIALIZATION FAILURE**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">The implementation will:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Break immediately with module errors</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Fail to read environment variables</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Cause connection pool exhaustion in production</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Result in import errors that prevent compilation</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Cause performance issues and connection failures</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Fail with &quot;HTTP connection string is not supported&quot; errors when using local URLs</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## USEFUL COMMANDS</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># After changing schema</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> generate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">              # Regenerate client (--no-engine flag no longer needed)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Push schema to database (no migrations)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> db</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> push</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Test database connection</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> run</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> db:test</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Open visual database editor</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> run</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> db:studio</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Create and apply migrations (for production)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> migrate</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> dev</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> --name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> your_migration_name</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## TESTING WORKFLOW</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">After setup, test with these steps:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Test database connection**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   npm run db:test</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   Should create a demo user and display it.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Open Prisma Studio**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   npm run db:studio</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   Visual interface at </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`localhost:5555`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to view/edit data.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Test API routes**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   # Create a user via API</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   curl -X POST http://localhost:3000/api/users </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     -H </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Content-Type: application/json&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> \</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     -d </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&#x27;{&quot;email&quot;:&quot;test@example.com&quot;,&quot;name&quot;:&quot;Test User&quot;}&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   # Get all users</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   curl http://localhost:3000/api/users</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **View in browser**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   Open </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`localhost:3000`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to see users displayed on the homepage.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## AI MODEL RESPONSE TEMPLATE</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">When asked about Prisma + Nuxt implementation, you MUST:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ONLY use code patterns from this guide</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> NEVER suggest deprecated approaches</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS use the exact patterns shown above</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS include </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`/client`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in import paths</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS add </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import &quot;dotenv/config&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to prisma.config.ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS add </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import &quot;dotenv/config&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to test scripts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS create the Prisma client in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`server/utils/db.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (Nuxt auto-imports)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">8.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS create the test script at </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`scripts/test-database.ts`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">9.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS add npm scripts for </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:test`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> and </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:studio`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">10.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS include error handling in API routes using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`createError`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">11.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS use the auto-imported </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> instance in server routes</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">12.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@prisma/adapter-pg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> with </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`PrismaPg`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> and </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`adapter`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> property</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">13.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> NEVER include </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`url`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in the datasource block of schema.prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">14.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> NEVER include </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`engine`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> property in prisma.config.ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">15.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS ask the user to run </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`npx prisma init --db --output ./generated`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **manually in their own terminal**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (this command is interactive and requires user input for region and project name)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">16.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS wait for user confirmation after they run the interactive </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma init --db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> command before proceeding</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">17.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> NEVER attempt to run interactive commands yourself - ask the user to do it</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">18.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> NEVER use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma+postgres://`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> URLs - ONLY </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`postgres://`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> TCP URLs</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">19.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> NEVER manually invent or fabricate DATABASE_URL values</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">20.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ALWAYS let Prisma generate the </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> file with the real DATABASE_URL (and ensure it&#x27;s correct type)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">21.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> VERIFY your response against ALL the patterns shown here before responding</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Remember: There are NO EXCEPTIONS to these rules. Every requirement is MANDATORY for the setup to work.</span></span></code></pre></div></figure></div><div class="flex flex-row flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-4 border-t pt-6 text-sm"><a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://github.com/prisma/docs/edit/main/apps/docs/content/docs/ai/prompts/nuxt.mdx" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring border bg-fd-secondary
